<P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Statement of Alex Wynaendts, CEO </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B></B>&#147;<B></B>AEGON&#146;s first quarter results demonstrate the strength of our business during what continues to be an uncertain economic
environment. We saw improved underlying earnings and net income, as well as strong deposits and new life sales. AEGON&#146;s excess capital continues to provide the substantial buffer we feel is necessary at this time. During the first three months
of the year, deposits totaled EUR 7.8 billion, a substantial increase of 16% over the previous quarter and a further indication of the continued strength of AEGON&#146;s franchise. In the current environment, we decided to reprice fixed annuities in
the United States as well as immediate annuities in the United Kingdom. These actions led to a modest decline in sales in the quarter and a lower value of new business overall. Impairments to AEGON&#146;s investment portfolio showed consecutive
improvement, continuing their downward trend. All in all, we are pleased with these first results of 2010 as they confirm that our strategic priorities are the right ones.&#148; </FONT></P>

<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Received 9th provincial license in China</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Portfolio
review </B> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">AEGON is continuing to assess its businesses to ensure they meet requirements in terms of earnings growth, cash flow potential,
return on capital and customer life cycle needs. As part of this review, AEGON earlier this year announced the sale of its funeral insurance business in the Netherlands for EUR 212 million. The transaction was completed on April&nbsp;1 and will
result in a modest book gain in the second quarter 2010. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Cost savings </B> </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">To improve returns from its businesses, AEGON implemented a number of measures to reduce operating expenses. As a result, operating expenses declined 4%
compared with the first quarter of 2009 to EUR 812&nbsp;million mainly driven by cost reductions, lower restructuring expenses and currency movements, partly offset by higher regulatory costs. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Operational excellence </B> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">AEGON
differentiates itself by competing on customer service levels and quality products and, in general, not on pricing. Though AEGON is already a cost-efficient provider, the company has identified possible further efficiencies, such as reducing the
number of administration platforms, reducing processing time and increasing productivity, while improving the level of customer service. AEGON is also investing in its web capabilities to further improve customer service levels, lower distribution
costs and improve communications with customers. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I></I><B>Capital preservation</B><I> </I> </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I></I>During the first quarter, a further EUR 0.1 billion in capital was released from AEGON&#146;s businesses, primarily the result of a reduction in
asset balances from run-off businesses. The release in the first quarter of 2010 was substantially lower than in previous quarters. <I> </I></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Manage AEGON as an international company </B> </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Starting with the first quarter of 2010, AEGON will report results from AEGON Asset Management separately within its &#145;New Markets&#146; segment.
AEGON Asset Management was launched at the beginning of October 2009 and brings together asset management businesses from around the world. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>AEGON&#146;S AMBITION </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">To be a global
leader in helping customers secure their financial futures </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>AEGON&#146;S STRATEGIC PRIORITIES </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="line-height:1px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:1pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" ALIGN="center">

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="82%"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="2%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="16%"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="middle"> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">OPERATIONAL HIGHLIGHTS</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="middle"> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right">

<IMG SRC="g19205g81r66.jpg" ALT="LOGO"></P>
 <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" align="left">&nbsp;</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="line-height:1px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:1pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Underlying earnings before tax </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">AEGON&#146;s underlying earnings before tax increased to EUR 488&nbsp;million in the first quarter, a considerable improvement compared with the same
period last year, the result mainly of improved financial markets and cost savings measures. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In the <B>Americas</B>, underlying earnings
totaled USD 524&nbsp;million compared with a loss of USD 189&nbsp;million a year earlier. A recovery in equity markets and higher account balances and investment income led to better results. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Underlying earnings in the <B>Netherlands</B> increased to EUR 104&nbsp;million, up from EUR 72&nbsp;million in the first quarter last year. This
increase was mainly the result of higher investment income and lower operating expenses. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In the <B>United Kingdom</B>, underlying earnings
amounted to GBP 25&nbsp;million, a substantial increase from GBP 9&nbsp;million in the first quarter 2009, as investment income and fees benefitted from the improvement in equity and bond markets. Technical results also improved, as a result of
lower than expected claims. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Underlying earnings from <B>New Markets</B> increased to EUR 46&nbsp;million due to improved results from most
operating units and the inclusion for the first time of earnings from AEGON Asset Management. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Expenses for AEGON&#146;s holding company
increased in the first quarter 2010 to EUR 69&nbsp;million, primarily a result of higher funding costs. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Fair value items </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In the first quarter, fair value items showed an overall underperformance of EUR 16&nbsp;million, a significant improvement compared with last year.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Overperformance in the Netherlands is mainly a result of movements in the fair value of guarantees and related hedges. This was offset by an
under-performance in the Americas, due primarily to a decline in the value of both the company&#146;s macro equity hedge and its real estate related assets. In addition, a further narrowing of AEGON&#146;s own credit spread and fair value movements
of derivatives resulted in a loss of EUR 27&nbsp;million for the holding company. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Gains on investments </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In the first quarter, realized gains on investments amounted to EUR 126 million. In both the United States and the Netherlands, gains were related
primarily to the sale of bonds, driven by asset and liability management. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Impairment charges </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Compared with the first quarter of 2009, net impairments decreased sharply to EUR 150&nbsp;million, their lowest level for seven quarters, though still
above AEGON&#146;s long-term average expectations. Included are impairments related to the US-based financial services provider Ambac of EUR 43 million. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Run-off businesses </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">AEGON&#146;s run-off
businesses in the Americas recorded a loss for the first quarter of EUR 60&nbsp;million, in line with the company&#146;s expectations. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Income tax </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Tax charges in the first
quarter amounted to EUR 39&nbsp;million and included a EUR 43&nbsp;million tax benefit related to cross-border intercompany reinsurance transactions between the United States and Ireland. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>New life sales </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Increased new life sales
in the Americas and Central&nbsp;&amp; Eastern Europe were more than offset by decreases in the United Kingdom and Spain, resulting in total new life sales for the first quarter of 2010 of EUR 538 million. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Deposits </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Gross deposits, excluding
run-off businesses, rose 3% to EUR 7.8 billion compared with the first quarter last year. US pensions and third-party asset management showed increases, while deposits of fixed annuities were significantly lower following repricing. All country
units recorded net deposits in the first quarter, which totaled EUR 741&nbsp;million, excluding run-off businesses. The company&#146;s US pension business added a new bank distribution partner during the quarter, and accounted for the majority of
net deposits. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="line-height:1px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:1pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" ALIGN="center">

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="85%"></TD>

 <P STYLE="line-height:1px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:1pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" ALIGN="center">

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="82%"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="2%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="16%"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="middle"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="middle">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right">

<IMG SRC="g19205g81r66.jpg" ALT="LOGO"></P>
 <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" align="left">&nbsp;</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="line-height:1px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:1pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Value of new business </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">AEGON&#146;s value of new business declined to EUR 146&nbsp;million in the first quarter. Higher value of new business from the Netherlands and variable
annuities in Europe was more than offset by decreases in the United Kingdom, the Americas and Spain. In the United Kingdom immediate annuity sales and in the United States fixed annuity sales declined following repricing, while lower sales of risk
products led to a lower value of new business in Spain. AEGON&#146;s internal rate of return on new business increased to 19% in the first quarter, due to improvements in both the Americas and the Netherlands. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Revenue-generating investments </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Revenue-generating investments totaled EUR 388 billion, an increase of 7% compared with year-end 2009. The increase was due primarily to a strengthening
of the US dollar against the euro and improvements in market values. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Capital management </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">-</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">At the end of the first quarter, AEGON&#146;s core capital, excluding revaluation reserves, amounted to EUR 17 billion, or 74% of the company&#146;s
total capital base</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">6,7</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">-</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Revaluation reserves at March&nbsp;31, 2010 amounted to a negative EUR 474&nbsp;million, a significant improvement from year-end 2009 levels, mainly due to an increase
in the value of fixed income securities. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">-</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Shareholders&#146; equity improved to EUR 14.5 billion as a result of improved revaluation reserves, strengthening of the US dollar against the euro and net income of
EUR 372&nbsp;million for the first quarter. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">-</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">At March&nbsp;31, 2010, AEGON&#146;s Insurance Group Directive (IGD) capital surplus totaled EUR 7.0 billion, equivalent to a solvency ratio of 205%.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">-</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Excess capital above AA capital adequacy requirements totaled EUR 3.7 billion. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Risk management </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Standard&nbsp;&amp;
Poor&#146;s has upgraded its assessment of AEGON&#146;s enterprise risk management (ERM) framework to &#145;strong&#146;, reflecting significant advances the company has made in developing its risk management framework and the fact that this
framework is now fully embedded in its business. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">AEGON is engaged in the process of obtaining the European&#146;s Commission&#146;s final
consent to the terms relating to AEGON&#146;s participation in the capital support program of the Dutch government at the end of 2008.&nbsp;In&nbsp;November 2009, AEGON submitted a plan, through the Dutch Ministry of Finance, to the European
Commission to demonstrate that its businesses are fundamentally sound and viable. This plan is a requirement for all financial institutions that received state support during the financial crisis. AEGON is not in a position to speculate about the
timing or final outcome of this process; nor to discuss any details relating to the process underway. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="line-height:1px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:1pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>

<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Gross deposits remain strong at USD 7.5 billion, helped by demand for pension products</B></FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Underlying earnings before tax </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Underlying earnings totaled USD 524&nbsp;million compared with a loss of USD 189&nbsp;million a year earlier. A recovery in equity markets and higher
account balances and investment income led to better results. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" ALIGN="center">

<TR>
<TD></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="3%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="97%"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="font-size:4px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px; margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS">&#161;
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></FONT></FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Earnings from Life&nbsp;&amp; Protection amounted to USD 194&nbsp;million, a slight decrease compared with the first quarter 2009, mainly driven by adverse claim experience in
the protection business.</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="8" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="font-size:4px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px; margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS">&#161;
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></FONT></FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Individual Savings&nbsp;&amp; Retirement earnings increased to USD 190&nbsp;million as variable annuities and mutual funds profited from a recovery in equity markets. Fixed
annuities, meanwhile, benefited from wider spreads.</FONT></TD></TR>

</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></FONT></FONT></P></TD>

<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Earnings from Employer Solutions&nbsp;&amp; Pensions increased to USD 86&nbsp;million, primarily the result of further business growth and improved margins.</FONT></TD></TR>

<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Life reinsurance earnings increased to USD 42&nbsp;million, as a result of a recovery in equity markets, improved mortality and higher investment income.</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>

<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="font-size:4px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px; margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS">&#161;
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></FONT></FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Earnings from AEGON&#146;s operations in Canada amounted to USD 11&nbsp;million, a decline compared with last year, mainly as a result of lower mortality
results.</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="8" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="font-size:4px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px; margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS">&#161;
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></FONT></FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Latin America, which represents AEGON&#146;s joint ventures in Brazil and Mexico, contributed USD 1&nbsp;million to earnings.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Net income </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net income from AEGON&#146;s
operations in the Americas amounted to USD 217&nbsp;million, a considerable improvement from the same quarter last year. This improvement was the result of substantially higher underlying earnings, realized gains on investments and a strong decline
in impairments. These factors more than offset an underperformance in fair value items and lower earnings from AEGON&#146;s run-off businesses. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The underperformance in fair value items totaled USD 120&nbsp;million, due primarily to a decline in the value of both the company&#146;s macro equity
hedge and its real estate related assets. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Realized gains on investments amounted to USD 33&nbsp;million in the first quarter this year, and
were related to corporate investment grade bonds sold in order to extend the average duration of assets held in some of AEGON&#146;s investment portfolios. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">At USD 191&nbsp;million, net impairments remain above AEGON&#146;s long-term expectations. Of the impairments during the first quarter, USD
60&nbsp;million was related to US financial firm Ambac. The majority of these impairments consisted of structured assets for which AEGON no longer values the Ambac guarantee. Of the total impairments, USD 151&nbsp;million was attributable to US
housing related assets. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">AEGON&#146;s run-off businesses in the Americas recorded a loss in the first quarter of USD 83&nbsp;million, in line
with expectations. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net income from AEGON&#146;s operations in the Americas included a tax benefit of USD 54&nbsp;million in the first quarter
as tax charges on underlying earnings were more than offset by tax benefits on both the company&#146;s non-underlying earnings and on cross-border intercompany reinsurance treaties. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Operating expenses </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating expenses
declined to USD 501&nbsp;million as a result of lower restructuring and employee benefit plan costs and the transfer of asset management activities to AEGON Asset Management. Adjusted operating expenses remained stable as continued cost savings
initiatives offset growth in the business. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Sales and deposits </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">New life sales increased 9% compared with the first quarter 2009 to USD 202 million. This was a result of growth across most of the company&#146;s
distribution channels, and particularly in the retail life insurance businesses across the Americas. New premium production for accident and health products declined to USD 184&nbsp;million however, as higher sales from worksite marketing were more
than offset by the effects of the closure of AEGON&#146;s automotive credit business in the United States in 2009. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="line-height:1px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:1pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" ALIGN="center">

<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="2%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="13%"></TD></TR>

<TD VALIGN="middle"> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right">

<IMG SRC="g19205g81r66.jpg" ALT="LOGO"></P>
 <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" align="left">&nbsp;</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="line-height:1px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:1pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Gross deposits excluding run-off businesses decreased 3% to USD 7.5 billion as higher pension, variable
annuity and mutual fund deposits were offset by lower fixed annuity deposits, following repricing. In addition, written pension sales were up strongly and a new bank distribution partner for retirement products was added during the quarter. Net
deposits excluding run-off businesses totaled USD 0.7 billion as pension and mutual fund inflows were partly offset by outflows from variable annuities in Canada and fixed annuities in the United States. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Value of new business </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Value of new
business declined to USD 71&nbsp;million despite higher margins on variable annuities and mutual funds. The reduction in the value of new business was primarily the result of lower fixed annuity sales and higher assumed reserve financing costs. The
internal rate of return for the quarter rose to 13%. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Revenue-generating assets </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Revenue-generating assets declined to USD 306 billion, as new money inflows and the effect of improved financial markets were offset by outflows from
AEGON&#146;s run-off businesses and the transfer of assets to AEGON Asset Management. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="line-height:1px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:1pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>

<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Underlying earnings before tax rise to EUR 104 million; all businesses contribute to increase</B></FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="8" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">o</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Net income rises to EUR 223&nbsp;million</B></FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="8" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">o</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>New life sales remain high at EUR 62&nbsp;million</B></FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Underlying earnings before tax </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Underlying earnings increased to EUR 104&nbsp;million, up from EUR 72&nbsp;million in the first quarter last year. This increase was mainly the result of
higher investment income and lower operating expenses. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" ALIGN="center">

<TR>
<TD></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="3%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="97%"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="font-size:4px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px; margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS">&#161;
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></FONT></FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Earnings from Life&nbsp;&amp; Savings increased to EUR 39&nbsp;million, mainly the result of improved margins on savings account balances.</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="8" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="font-size:4px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px; margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS">&#161;
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></FONT></FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Pension earnings of EUR 47&nbsp;million were the result of improved underwriting results, higher interest results and cost saving measures.</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="8" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="font-size:4px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px; margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS">&#161;
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></FONT></FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Non-life earnings improved to EUR 7&nbsp;million mainly as a result of lower costs.</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="8" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="font-size:4px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px; margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS">&#161;
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></FONT></FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Earnings from Distribution increased to EUR 11&nbsp;million, primarily the result of the sale last year of the loss-making brokerage activities.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Net income </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net income from AEGON&#146;s
operations in the Netherlands increased to EUR 223 million. The improvement was the result of higher underlying earnings, positive results on fair value items and lower impairment charges, partly offset by a decline in gains on investments and an
increase in tax charges. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Fair value items showed an overperformance of EUR 91&nbsp;million mainly as a result of movements in the fair value
of guarantees and related hedges. As a result of adjustments in the investment portfolio for asset and liability management purposes, realized gains on investments totaled EUR 96 million. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Operating expenses </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating expenses
declined 16% to EUR 182&nbsp;million in the first quarter, the result of cost saving initiatives implemented last year, as well as the transfer of asset management activities in the Netherlands to AEGON Asset Management. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Sales and deposits </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">New life sales of
EUR 62&nbsp;million were in line with the first quarter last year, as higher Individual life sales were offset by lower pension sales. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Following recent changes in government regulations, more of the disability insurance market in the Netherlands is now open to private sector insurers. As
a result, AEGON&#146;s accident&nbsp;&amp; health premium production rose to EUR 11&nbsp;million in the first quarter of this year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Value
of new business </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Higher volumes and margins in the life business as well as improved margins on pensions resulted in an increase in the
value of new business in the first quarter of 2010 to EUR 49 million. The internal rate of return amounted to 19% over the first three months of the year, driven mainly by a change in business mix. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Revenue-generating investments </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Revenue-generating investments were stable at EUR 70.9 billion, compared with the previous quarter. This was primarily the result of a combination of
lower risk-free interest rates and higher equity markets during the quarter and the transfer of third party assets to AEGON Asset Management. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="line-height:1px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:1pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" ALIGN="center">

<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS">&#161;

<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Underlying earnings before tax increase to GBP 25&nbsp;million as financial markets improve</B></FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="8" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE="font-size:4px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS">&#161;
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><B></B></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><B></B></FONT></FONT></B></FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Net income increases to GBP 20&nbsp;million</B></FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="8" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE="font-size:4px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS">&#161;
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><B></B></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><B></B></FONT></FONT></B></FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>New life sales down to GBP 235&nbsp;million, mainly the result of lower annuity sales</B></FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Underlying earnings before tax </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Underlying earnings before tax from AEGON&#146;s businesses in the United Kingdom increased to GBP 25&nbsp;million in the first quarter as a result of
improved financial markets and growth in the business. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" ALIGN="center">

<TR>
<TD></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="2%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="98%"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="font-size:4px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS">&#161;
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></FONT></FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Earnings from Life&nbsp;&amp; Protection increased to GBP 18&nbsp;million due to a strong performance from annuities and lower than expected claims in the employee benefit
business, which was closed last year.</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="8" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="font-size:4px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS">&#161;
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></FONT></FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Pension earnings increased to GBP 9&nbsp;million as the positive effects of improved equity and credit markets and further business growth were offset partly by higher expenses.
</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="8" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="font-size:4px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:WINGDINGS">&#161;
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"></FONT></FONT></FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">AEGON&#146;s distribution businesses benefited from improved market conditions, limiting their losses for the first quarter to GBP 2 million.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Net income </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net income in the first
quarter 2010 increased to GBP 20&nbsp;million mainly as a result of higher underlying earnings and a decline in impairments. Impairments totaled GBP 7&nbsp;million, their lowest level for five quarters. Fair value items made a positive contribution
on the back of stronger equity markets, while realized gains on investments decreased. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Operating expenses </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating expenses decreased 1% to GBP 95&nbsp;million as higher costs were offset by the transfer of asset management activities at the beginning of the
year to AEGON Asset Management. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Sales and deposits </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">New life sales decreased to GBP 235 million. Higher sales of pension and retirement products were offset by a decrease in sales of immediate annuities
following repricing and the impact of the closure of AEGON&#146;s employee benefit business in the United Kingdom in the second quarter last year. Also, the comparable quarter last year included existing AEGON group personal pension business that
was transferred internally to new group pension contracts. AEGON has decided not to include these rewrites as part of new business reporting in the future as this gives a clearer indication of new premium secured. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Value of new business </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">AEGON&#146;s
value of new business declined to GBP 12&nbsp;million as a result of repricing immediate annuities and the decision to adopt a more conservative investment strategy and invest new assets in gilts. The internal rate of return on new business was 11%.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Revenue-generating investments </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Revenue-generating investments amounted to GBP 53.6 billion as increases in both the general account and for account of policyholders investments were
offset by the transfer of third-party investments to AEGON Asset Management. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="line-height:1px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:1pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>NEW MARKETS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Underlying earnings before tax </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Underlying earnings before tax amounted to EUR 46&nbsp;million as a result of improved results in most units and the inclusion for the first time of
earnings from AEGON Asset Management. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="97%"></TD></TR>

<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Earnings from <B>Central&nbsp;&amp; Eastern Europe</B> increased to EUR 27&nbsp;million, as higher results from the life insurance business following strict underwriting and cost
savings were partly offset by lower earnings from the pension and non-life insurance businesses.</FONT></TD></TR>

<TD VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operations in <B>Asia</B> made a loss of EUR 6 million. Life insurance results were positively affected by the sale last year of AEGON&#146;s loss-making life insurance activities
in Taiwan. Individual Savings and Retirement Products recorded a loss as a result of the company&#146;s variable annuity business in Japan. In addition, results last year included earnings from AEGON&#146;s asset management operations. These
earnings are now reported separately.</FONT></TD></TR>

<TD VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Earnings from <B>Spain and France</B> increased to EUR 20&nbsp;million, mainly due to a higher contribution from La Mondiale in France.</FONT></TD></TR>

<TD VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Variable Annuities Europe</B> reported a loss of EUR 2&nbsp;million, while earnings from <B>AEGON Asset Management</B> amounted to EUR 7 million.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Net income </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net income from New Markets
increased in the first quarter to EUR 37&nbsp;million as a result of higher underlying earnings and lower tax charges. Net income for the same period last year had included an impairment on deferred tax assets in Taiwan, which resulted in an
exceptionally high effective tax rate. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Operating expenses </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating expenses amounted to EUR 133 million. The increase compared with last year is due to the inclusion of AEGON Asset Management in New Markets,
effective from the first quarter this year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Sales and deposits </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">New life sales for New Markets declined to EUR 66&nbsp;million in the first quarter. Sales growth in both Central&nbsp;&amp; Eastern Europe and China was
more than offset by lower sales of both recurring and single premiums in Spain. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In Spain, due to the difficult economic environment, total new life sales for AEGON in Spain declined by 33% in the first quarter of 2010 to EUR 37 million.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Gross deposits from New Markets increased 47% to EUR 1.6 billion primarily as a result of higher third-party asset management inflows. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Value of new business </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">New Markets&#146;
value of new business amounted to EUR 31 million. Higher contributions from Central&nbsp;&amp; Eastern Europe, AEGON&#146;s European variable annuity business and the company&#146;s operations in China were more than offset by a decline in the value
of new business in Spain. The internal rate of return remained high. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Revenue-generating investments </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Revenue-generating investments increased to EUR 28.2 billion, driven by the inclusion for the first time of AEGON&#146;s Asset Management and off-shore
bond business in Dublin and a further improvement in financial markets. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">PVNBP: Present Value New Business Premium. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">a)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The calculation of the IGD (Insurance Group Directive) capital surplus and ratio are based on Solvency I capital requirements on IFRS for entities within the EU (Pillar
I for AEGON UK), and local regulatory solvency measurements for non-EU entities. Specifically, required capital for the life insurance companies in the US is calculated as two times the upper end of the Company Action Level range (200%)&nbsp;as
applied by the National Association of Insurance Commissioners in the US. The calculation of the IGD ratio excludes the available and required capital of the UK With-Profit funds. In the UK solvency surplus calculation the local regulator only
allows the available capital number of the With-Profit funds included in overall local available capital to be equal to the amount of With-Profit funds&#146; required capital. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD VALIGN="middle"> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">About AEGON</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="middle"></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="line-height:1px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:1pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">As an international life insurance, pension and investment company based in The Hague, AEGON has
businesses in over twenty markets in the Americas, Europe and Asia. AEGON companies employ approximately 28,000 people and have more than 40&nbsp;million customers across the globe. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><U>Cautionary note regarding non-GAAP measures </U></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">This press release includes certain non-GAAP financial measures: underlying earnings before tax and value of new business. The reconciliation of
underlying earnings before tax to the most comparable IFRS measure is provided in Note 3 &#147;Segment information&#148; of our Condensed consolidated interim financial statements. Value of new business is not based on IFRS, which are used to report
AEGON&#146;s quarterly statements and should not viewed as a substitute for IFRS financial measures. AEGON believes that these non-GAAP measures, together with the IFRS information, provide a meaningful measure for the investment community to
evaluate AEGON&#146;s business relative to the businesses of our peers. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><U>Local currencies and constant currency exchange rates
</U></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">This press release contains certain information about our results and financial condition in USD for the Americas and GBP for the United
Kingdom, because those businesses operate and are managed primarily in those currencies. Certain comparative information presented on a constant currency basis eliminates the effects of changes in currency exchange rates. None of this information is
a substitute for or superior to financial information about us presented in EUR, which is the currency of our primary financial statements. </FONT></P>

reliance on these forward-looking statements, which merely reflect company expectations at the time of writing. Actual results may differ materially from expectations conveyed in forward-looking statements due to changes caused by various risks and
